class="boom-mark-news-wrap-article-page"><a data-newsid="582265" data-url="/kerala/daily-cases-bounce-to-breach-10k-mark-for-first-time-in-kerala-582265" class="bookmark-news-item"><i class="mob-margin-auto"><div class="story-icon-cover"><div addthis:url="/kerala/daily-cases-bounce-to-breach-10k-mark-for-first-time-in-kerala-582265" addthis:title="Daily cases bounce to breach 10K mark for first time in Kerala" class="addthis_inline_share_toolbox"></div></div></div></div><div id="left_level_2" class=" hide"></div><div class="story-text"><div class="details-story-wrapper-inline"><div class="details-story-wrapper"><div class="content details-content-story"><div class="story"><p>Thiruvananthapuram: In a first, Kerala on Wednesday reported more than 10,000 new Covid-19 cases at 10,606.<br></p><p>One reason why there has been a huge spike in the number of cases is because as many as 73,816 samples were tested, the highest so far.  </p><p>A statement issued here by state Health Minister K.K. Shailaja said that the day also witnessed 6,161 recoveries.  </p><p>"At present, there are 92,161 active cases in the state, while 1,60,253 persons have so far been cured of the disease," said Shailaja.  </p><p>The state also reported 22 deaths in the past 24 hours, taking Kerala\'s Covid death toll to 906.  </p><p>Across the state, 2,67,834 people are under observation, including 29,503 in hospitals. There are 720 hotspots in the state at present.</p></div></div></div><div data-label="show-full" data-category="news-details" class="show-more-button-details-story track-click"><a
